80a5(mdo sde): sems dpa' chen po rnams yongs su gzung ba'i phyir bzhugs te/ gzhon nu khyod de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas la don
80a6(mdo sde): 'di zhu bar sems pa legs so// gzhon nu khyod kyi zhus pa bzang ste/ spobs pa dge'o// de'i phyir gzhonu khyod legs par rab tu nyon la yid la zung shig dang bsha
80a7(mdo sde): sems rtse gcig tu rna ba blags te sems bsdus la soms shig dang / don de ngas khyod la bshad de// de nas rgyal po gzugs can snying po'i sras khye'u rin chen zla
80a8(mdo sde): bas bcom ldan 'das la leg so zhes gsol nas/ bcom ldan 'das la ltar nyan pa dang / bcom ldan 'das kyis de la 'di skad ces bka' stsal to// gzhon
80b1(mdo sde): sangs rgyas kyi zhing 'di nas/ shar phyogs su sangs rgyas kyi zhing bye ba khrag khrig 'bum phrag dpag tu med/ grangs med/ bsam gyis mi khyab/ gzhal du med pa skyed
80b2(mdo sde): 'das pa na/ 'jig rten gyi khams mya ngan med pa zhes bya ba zhig yod do// 'jig rten gyi khams mya ngan med pa zhes bya ba de/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing dpag tu med pa ji snyed
80b3(mdo sde): cig 'das pa na yod ce na/ gzhon nu dper na/ stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams 'di srid pa'i rtse mo'i bar du byems yongs su gang bar gyur la/
80b4(mdo sde): de nas mi la la zhig gis bye ma de las 'bru re re nas blangs shing shar phyogs kyi sangs rgyas zhing re rer 'bru re 'jog par byed pa de lta bu'i tshul gyis bye ma de thams
80b5(mdo sde): cad shar phyogasu yongs su zad cing / yongs su gtugs par gyur kyang / sangs rgyas kyi zhing de dag gis tshad dam mtha' rtogs par mi nus pa'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing
80b6(mdo sde): bye ba khrag khrig 'bum phrag dpag tu med/ grangs med pa de snyed 'das pa na/ 'jig rten gyi khams mya ngan med pa zhes bya ba zhig yod do// 'jig rten gyi kham
80b7(mdo sde): de yang lag 'thil ltar mnyam par gyur pa/ rin po che sna bdun gyis legs par brgyan pa/ gser gyis gzhir 'dug cig mig dmangs ris su bris pa/
80b8(mdo sde): rin po che'i shing ljon pas brgyan pa/ sems can dmyal ba dang / dud 'gro'i skye gnas dang / yid dgas dang / lha ma yin gyi tshogs rnams med pa dang / rtswa dang /
81a1(mdo sde): shing skam dang / tsher ma dang / rdo dang / gseg ma dang / gyo mo dag med pa dang / ngam grog dang / g.yangs med pa dang / me tog sil ma dag bkra
81a2(mdo sde): pa yin te/ de na de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas dpal bzang po zhes bya ba da ltar bzhugs shing 'tshol ba zhes te/
81a3(mdo sde): byang chub sems dpa'i tshogs kyis bskor cing / byang chub sems dpas 'dun gyis bltas pa/ rig pa dang zhabasu ldan pa/ bde bar gshegs pa/ 'jig rten
81a4(mdo sde): mkhyen pa/ skyes bu 'dul ba'i kha lo bsgyur ba/ bla na med pa/ lha dang mi rnams kyi ston pa sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das skyes bu chen po'i mtshan sum cu rtsa gnyis kyis
81a5(mdo sde): brgyan pa'i ska/ gser legs par gtsos shing / legs par dul ba lta bu/ rin po che'i rgyan legs par bkod pa bzhin du/ 'khor gyi nang na mdzes par zhugs
81a6(mdo sde): shing / thog mar dge ba/ bar du dge ba/ tha mar dge ba'i chos ston to// 'di skad ces kyang ston to// 'di ltar sa'i khams ni med par mi 'gyur ro// de bzhin du
81a7(mdo sde): chu'i khams dang / me'i khams dang / rlung gi khams dang / skye dgu'i bdag po tshangs pa dang / gzugs dang / tsher ba dang / 'du shes dang / 'du byed dang /
81a8(mdo sde): rnam par shes pa med par mi 'gyur ro// zhes ston to// gzhon nu gzhan yang de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas dpal
81b1(mdo sde): bzang po bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mngon par sangs rgyas nas ni skal pa bye ba phrag drug bcu lon no// gzhon nu gzhan yang sangs rgyas
81b2(mdo sde): kyi zhing de ni nyin mo dang / mtshan mo'i ming yang med de/ 'dzam bu'i gling gi brtse ba'i thabs 'dis dper bya ba ni ma gtogs so// sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad
81b3(mdo sde): kyang / rtag tu de bzhin gshegs pa de'i 'od kyis snang bar 'dug go// gzhon nu de bzhin gshegs pa de chos bstan pa re res kyang / sems can bye ba khrag khrig
81b4(mdo sde): phrag 'bum dpag tu med pa dag mi skye ba'i chos la dgod par mdzad do// bzod pa dang po dang / bzod pa gnyis pa dang / bzod pa gsum pa la ni de'i nyis 'gyur
81b5(mdo sde): dgod par mdzad do// gzhon nu gzhan yang de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas de'i sngon gyi smon lam gyi stobs bskyed
81b6(mdo sde): pas/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing gzhan dag na/ gang dag sngon gyi rgyal ba rnams la lhag par bya ba byas shing dge ba'i rtsa ba bskyed pa'i sems can dag gi lus la
81b7(mdo sde): 'od kyis rig par de dag kyang mi skye ba'i chos bzod pa thob po// gzhon nu gzhan yang rigs kyi bu 'am/ rigs kyi bu mo yang rung de bzhin gshegs pa dgra
81b8(mdo sde): bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas dpal bzang po'i de'i mtshan thos nas/ bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub las phyir mi ldog par
82a1(mdo sde): 'gyur ro// gzhon nu 'di nas lho phyogasu sangs rgyas kyi zhing bye ba khrag khrig 'bum phrag grangs med pa snga ma ji snyed pa de snyed 'das
82a2(mdo sde): pa na/ 'jig rten gyi khams dga' ba zhes bya ba zhig yod do// lag 'thil ltar mnyam pa zhes bya ba nas snga ma bzhin du sbyar ro// de na de bzhin gshegs
82a3(mdo sde): pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas tsan dan dpal zhes bya ba da ltar bzhugs shing 'tshe la bzhes te/ byang chub sems dpa' bskor
82a4(mdo sde): cing / byang chub sems dpa'i mdun gyis ltas pa la/ thog mar dge ba/ bar du dge ba/ tha mar dge ba'i chos ston to// zhes bya ba nas rnam par shes pa
82a5(mdo sde): med par mi 'gyur ro// zhes bya ba'i bar du snga ma bzhin du sbyar ro// gzhon nu de la ji snyam du sems/ ci'i phyir de bzhin gshegs pa de tsan dan dpal zhes
82a6(mdo sde): bya ba zhe na/ gzhon nu de bzhin gshegs pa de ni sangs rgyas kyi zhing de thams cad tsan dan gyi khang pa brtsegs pa yongs su khyab pas na/ de'i phyir de bzhin
82a7(mdo sde): gshegs pa de'i mtshan can dan dpal zhes bya'o// / gzhan yang rigs kyi bu 'am/ rigs kyi bu mo yang rung de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par
82a8(mdo sde): rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas de'i mtshan thos na/ bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub las phyir mi ldog par 'gyur ro// gzhon nu dri nas nub phyogasu/
82b1(mdo sde): sangs rgyas kyi zhing bye ba khrag khrig 'bum phrag grangs med pa snga ma ji srid 'das pa na/ 'jig rten gyi khams bzang po zhes bya ba zhig yod do// lag mthil ltar/
82b2(mdo sde): mnyam par gyur pa zhes bya ba nas snga ma bzhin du sbyar te/ ji ltar gong du bstan pa bzhin no// de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs
82b3(mdo sde): snang mtha' yas zhes bya ba da ltar bzhugs shing 'tshe la bzhes te/ byang chub sems dpa' yongs su bskor cing / byang chub sems dpa' 'dun gyis bltas pa la/
82b4(mdo sde): thog mar dge ba/ bar du dge ba/ tha mar dge ba'i chos ston to// 'di skad bdag kyang ston to zhes bya ba nas/ rnam par shes pa med par mi 'gyur ro// zhes bya ba'i bar
82b5(mdo sde): du snga ma bzhin du sbyar ro// gzhon nu gzhan yang rigs kyi bu 'am/ rigs kyi bu mo yang rung / de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs
82b6(mdo sde): de'i mtshan thos na/ bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub las phyir mi ldog par 'gyur zhing / 'od de yang nyam su myong ngo // gzhon nu 'di nas byang phyogs
82b7(mdo sde): su sangs rgyas kyi zhing bye ba khrag khrig 'bum phrag grangs med pa snga ma ji snyed 'das pa na/ 'jig rten gyi khams khrug mod ces bya ba yod de/ lag mthil ltar
82b8(mdo sde): mnyam par gyur pa zhes bya ba nas/ thams cad snga ma bzhin du sbyararo// de na de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rtog gi dpal
83a1(mdo sde): zhes bya ba da ltar bzhugs shing mtshol bzhes te/ byang chub sems dpas yongs su bskor cing / byang chub sems dpa' mdun gyi ltas pa
83a2(mdo sde): la chos ston to// zhes bya ba nas/ rnam par shes pa med par mi 'gyur ro// zhes bya ba'i bar du snga ma bzhin du sbyar ro// gzhon nu gzhan yang rigs kyi bu 'am/
83a3(mdo sde): rigs kyi bu mo yang rung / de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas de'i mtshan thos nas/ bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i
83a4(mdo sde): byang chub las phyir mi ldog par 'gyur zhing / lha dang bcas pa'i 'jig rten yin gyi khams rgyal mtshan lta bur 'gyur ro// gzhon nu 'di nas shar lho'i phyogs
83a5(mdo sde): mtshamasu sangs rgyas kyi zhing bye ba khrag khrig 'bum phrag grangs med pa de snyed 'das na/ 'jig rten gyi khams zla ba snang ba zhes bya ba zhig yod do// lag
83a6(mdo sde): mthil ltar mnyam pa zhes bya ba nas snga ma bzhin du sbyar ro// gzhon nu de la ji snyam du sems/ ci'i phyir 'jig rten gyi khams zla ba snang ba zhes bya ba zhe
83a7(mdo sde): na/ 'jig rten gyi khams de thams cad de bzhin gshegs pa de'i 'od kyi snang bar bya bas na/ de'i phyir 'jig rten gyi khams de zla ba snang ba zhes bya'o//
83a8(mdo sde): de na de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas mya ngan med pa'i dpal zhes bya ba de ltar bzhugs shing 'tshel bzhes te/
83b1(mdo sde): byang chub sems dpas yongasu bskor cing / byang chub sems dpas mdun gyis ltas pa la/ chos ston to zhes bya ba nas/ rnam par shes pa med par mid 'gyuraro//
83b2(mdo sde): zhes bya ba'i bar du snga ma bzhin du sbyar ro// rigs kyi bu 'am/ rigs kyi bu mo yang rung / de'i mtshan thos na med po yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub las myi ldog

83b5(mdo sde): yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rin po che'i mchod sdod zhes bya ba da ltar bzhags shing 'tsho la bzhes te/ byang chub sems dpas yongs su bskor cing //
83b6(mdo sde): byang chub sems dpas 'dun gyis ltas pa la chos ston to// zhes bya ba nas/ rnam par shes pa med par mi 'gyur ro zhes bya ba'i bar du snga ma bzhin du sbyar ro// /

83b8(mdo sde): na rin chen lngar mngon par 'phags par 'gyur ro// gzhon nu 'di nas nub byang gi phyogs mtsham su sangs rgyas kyi zhing bye ba khrag khrig 'bum phrag grangs med
84a1(mdo sde): pa de snyed 'das pa na/ 'jig rten gyi khams sgra ldan zhes bya ba zhig yod de/ lag 'brel ltar mnyam par gyur pa zhes bya ba nas/ snga ma
84a2(mdo sde): bzhin du bsgyur ro// gzhon nu de ji snyam du sems/ ci'i phyir 'jig rten gyi khams de sgra ldan zhes bya ba zhes na/ 'jig rten gyi khams de sgra 'di lta bu dag dang ldan
84a3(mdo sde): te/ 'di lta ste/ sangs rgyas kyi sgra dang / chos kyi sgra dang / dge 'dun gyi sgra dang / stong pa nyid kyi sgra dang / mtshan ma med pa'i sgra dang / smon pa med pa'i sgra dang / sbyin pa/
84a4(mdo sde): dang / tshul khrims dang / bzod pa dang / brtson 'grus dang / bsam gtan dang / shes rab kyi sgra dang / rnam par grol ba'i ye shes gzigs pa'i sgra rnams dang ldanano//

84a8(mdo sde): mo gang yang rung ba'i mtshan thos nas/ bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub las phyir mi ldog par 'gyur zhing / me tog ltar mi dge ba'i chos rnams
84b1(mdo sde): kyis kyang gosmra bar mi 'gyur ro// gzhon nu 'di nas byang shar gyi phyogs mtsham su sangs rgyas kyi zhing bye ba khrag khrig 'bum phrag grangs med pa de snyed 'das pa na/ 'jig
84b2(mdo sde): rten gyi khams bde ldan zhes bya ba zhig yod de/ 'byor pa dang rgyas pa dang / bde ba dang / lo legs pa dang / skye bo dang / mi mang pos gang zhing / lag 'thil ltar

84b7(mdo sde): cad la mkhas shing pha rol tu phyin pa'i shes pa yang yongs su 'dzin par 'gyur ro// gzhon nu 'di nas 'og gi phyogs su sangs rgyas kyi zhing bye ba khrag khrig 'bum

85a1(mdo sde): gyi khams de yangs pa dang ldan pa zhes bya zhe na/ 'jig rten gyi khams de lags mthil ltar mnyam par gyur pa/ ri med cing khor yug dang /

85a8(mdo sde): bcan zhes bya ba de sangs rgyas kyi zhing dpag tu med pa de snyed cig 'das pa na yod cen/ gzhon nu 'di lta ste/ stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams

86a7(mdo sde): pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas spyod pa dang / yon tan phun sum tshogs pa dang / ye shes phun sum tshogs pa dang / tshul khrims dang ting nge 'dzin dang /
86a8(mdo sde): shes rab dang / rnam par grol ba dang / rnam par grol ba'i ye shes gzigs pa phun sum tshogs pa dang ldan pa de dag gi mtshan thos na/ bla na med pa yang dag
86b1(mdo sde): par rdzogs pa'i byang chub las phyir mi ldog par 'gyuraro// gzhon nu sngon byung ba 'das pa'i dus na/ bskal pa grangs med pas kyang ches grangs med pa/ yun ring

100a6(mdo sde): ldan 'das gnyan yod na rgyal bu rgyal byed kyi tshal mgon med zas sprin gyi kun dga' ra ba na/ dge slong lnga stong thams pa'i dge slong gi dge 'dun chen po dang /

100a8(mdo sde): las langs te/ bla gos phrag pa gcig tu gzar nas/ pus mo g.yas pa'i lha nga sa la gtsugs te/ bcom ldan 'das ga la ba der log su thal mo sbyar

180a3(mdo sde): pa'i chos dang ldan pa'i phyir dang / lhun gyis grub cing rnam par mi rtog par de'i bya ba de rtag tu 'byung ngo // 'jam dpal de bzhin du de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom
180a4(mdo sde): pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas kyang srid pa'i rgya mtsho las mngon par 'phags te/ chos kyi dbyings kyi na mkha'i spyod yul la gnas nas/ ye shes kyi 'od zer bye ba
180a5(mdo sde): khrag khrig 'bum phrag grangs med pa btang bas/ phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten gyi khams rab 'byams thams cad snang ba'i sbyin pa mdzad cing / sems can thams cad kyi
180a6(mdo sde): ma rig mun pa mun nag dang / rab rib dang / ling tog rnams rnam par sel bar mdzad/ nyon mongs pa'i 'dam rdzab dang / rnyog pa thams cad bskems par mdzad/ yun
180a7(mdo sde): ring po nas gnyid kyis logs pa'i sems can gyi khams ni sad par mdzad/ sems can thams cad kyi dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad ni skye bar mdzad/ sems can thams cad kyi
180a8(mdo sde): dge ba'i rtsa ba'i tshogs thams cad ni yongs su smin par mdzad/ dge ba'i rtsa ba'i sgo thams cad ni rab tu 'joms par mdzad de/ dus gcig tu de'i mdzad pa thams cad 'byung
180b1(mdo sde): yang / gnas nas mi g.yo zhing / 'jam dpal de bzhin gshegs pa ni mi rtog rnam par mi rtog ste/ 'on kyang ma 'dres pa'i chos dang ldan pa'i phyir/ lhun gyis grub pa
180b2(mdo sde): rnam par mi rtog par de'i mdzad pa de lta bu de 'byung ngo // 'jam dpal de ltar de bzhin gshegs pa ni lhun gyis grub cing rnam par mi rtog par sems can yongs su smin pa/
180b3(mdo sde): mdzad pa'i gnas kyang dge ba'i gshes gnyen gyis yongs su zin pa las byung ngo // 'jam dpal dge ba'i gshes gnyen gyis yongs su zin pa'i byang chub sems dpa' ni//
180b4(mdo sde): chos rab tu rnam par 'byed cing / dpyod pa la mkhas par 'gyur te/ de chos rnams la 'di ltar spyod do// mig ni gzugs kyi dmigs pa'i rgyu ma yin/ gzugs kyang
180b5(mdo sde): mig gi dmigs pa'i rgyu ma yin la/ dmigs pa'i rgyu rkyen nyid kyis kyang rnam par shes pa 'byung ste/ rnam par shes pa yang mig las kyang ma byung / gzugs las kya
180b6(mdo sde): ma byung zhing rnam par shes pa de ni/ byung nas zhig la zhu zhing mi gnas pa'o// rna ba dang / sna dang / lce dang lus kyang de bzhin no// yid kyang chos kyi rkyen ma yin zhing / chos
180b7(mdo sde): kyang yid kyi rkyen ma yin la/ dmigs pa'i rgyu rkyen nyid kyis kyang rnam par shes pa byung ste/ rnam par shes pa de ni yid las kyang ma byung / chos rnams las kyang ma byung zhing
180b8(mdo sde): yid kyi rnam par shes pa de ni byung nas kyang zhig la/ zhu zhing mi gnas pa'o// de bzhin du dge ba'i rtsa ba yang byang chub kyi rkyen ma yin/ byang chub kyang dge ba'i rtsa ba ma yin/
181a1(mdo sde): mod kyi/ dge ba'i rtsa ba de yang byang chub kyi rkyen las dmigs pa las/ sems bskyeb rnams kyis skyes te/ de dag kyang skyes nas
181a2(mdo sde): zhig cing zhum la mi gnas pa'o// de la sems gang gis dge ba'i rtsa ba mngon par 'du sa byas pa dang / sems gang gis byang chub kyi yongs su bsngos pa de gnyis ni phan tshun
181a3(mdo sde): mi sbyor ro// dper na/ mi ni gang nas kyang mi 'ong gang du yang mi 'gro'o// 'on kyang rgyu dang / rkyen gyis 'bar ro// 'jam dpal de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa'i shes rab
181a4(mdo sde): kyi me 'bar ba yang gang nas kyang mi 'ong gang du yang mi 'gro ste/ 'on kyang dge ba'i rtsa ba'i rgyu la brten nas/ byang chub sems dpa'i shes rab kyi me 'bar te shes pa de lta bu
181a5(mdo sde): dang ldan pa de ni bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya'o// 'jam dpal de ltar na dge ba'i gshes gnyen rnams ni yon tan rgya
181a6(mdo sde): mtsho tshad med pa yin no// 'jam dpal rigs kyi bu 'am/ rigs kyi bu mo gang la la zhig gis phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi rdul snyed kyi/ sangs rgyas
181a7(mdo sde): bcom ldan 'das byang chub sems dpa' dang / bcas nyan thos dang bcas pa rnams la rtag par nyin gcig bzhin du zhal zas ro brgya dang ldan pa dang / lha'i na bza' dag
181a8(mdo sde): phul la/ de ltar 'bul ba bskal pa gang ga'i klung gi bye ma snyed du phul zhing / de bzhin gshegs pa de dag yongs su mya ngan las 'das nas/ de bzhin gshegs re/
181b1(mdo sde): de'i phyir yang phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten gyi khams rab 'byams thams cad du 'jig rten gyi khams re rer yang mchod rten 'dzam bu'i chu bo'i gser las byas pa/ nor bu
181b2(mdo sde): rin po che glog gi sgron mas sbas pa/ nor bu rin po che 'od thams cad bsdus pa'i stegs bus yongs su bskor ba/ nor bu dang / mu tig dang / nor bu rin po che'i 'phreng
181b3(mdo sde): bas mdzes par byas pa dang / gdugs dang / rgyal mtshan dang / bden bsgreng ba/ dril bu g.yer ka'i dra ba'i bres pa/ tsan dan sbrul gyi snying po'i byug pa byug pa/
181b4(mdo sde): nor bu rin po che dbang gi rgyal po'i dra bas khebs par byas pa/ phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi rdul snyed dag byas ste/ mchod rten de dag la stong gsum
181b5(mdo sde): gyi stong chen po'i tshad tsam gyis lha'i na bza' dag dang / gdugs kyi sprin dag dang / rgyal mtshan gyi sprin dag dang / ba dan gyi sprin dag dang / me tog gi sprin dag dang / spos
181b6(mdo sde): kyi sprin dag dang / nor bu rin po che dbang gi rgyal po'i sprin dag dang / yid bzhin gyi nor bu rin po che'i sprin dag gis gtor/ mngon par gtor la/ nyin gcig bzhin de
181b7(mdo sde): ltar mchod cing bskal pa gang ga'i klung gi bye ma snyed du mchod la/ sems can gzhan dpag tu med grangs med pa dag kyang mchod pa de nyid 'god pas/ 'jam dpal rig
181b8(mdo sde): kyi bu'am/ rigs kyi bu mo gzhan dag gis de bzhin gshegs pa'i yon tan dang / ye shes bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i yul la 'jug pa brtan pa'i chos rnams grangs 'di
182a1(mdo sde): la than mos pa byed na/ 'di nyid de bas bsod nams ches grangs med par skyed do// 'jam dpal chos kyi rnam grangs 'di la mos pa'i byang chub
182a2(mdo sde): sems dpa' ni pha rol tu phyin pa bye ba khrag khrig 'bum phrag dpag tu med pa dag yongs su rdzogs par byed do// sa bye ba khrag khrig 'bum phrag dpag tu med grangs med pa dag gnan
182a3(mdo sde): to// bskal pa bye ba khrag khrig 'bum phrag grangs med pa btang bas/ grong dang / grong khyer dang / grong rdal dang / ljongs dang / rgyal po'i pho brang 'khor thams cad du mthong ba
182a4(mdo sde): sbyin par byed cing mun pa sel bar byed/ 'dam rdzab dang / rnyog pa thams cad skems par byed/ 2pad+ma rnams kyang 'byed par byed/ rtsa ba dang / shing gel ba dang / sman dang
182a5(mdo sde): nags tshal thams cad kyang skye bar byed/ sman thams cad kyang yongs su smin par byed/ las kyi gnas thams cad ni gnas par byed la/ chu klung dang / mtshe'u dang / mtsho
182a6(mdo sde): bran thams cad la yang dus gcig tu snang ba thob par 'gyur yang / gnas las kyang mi g.yo zhing / 'jam dpal nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor ni mi rtog rnam par mi rtog ste/ 'on
182a7(mdo sde): kyang ma 'dres pa'i ba'i chos dang ldan pa'i phyir lhun gyis grub cing rnam par mi rtog par de'i bya ba de rtag tu 'byung ngo // 'jam dpal de bzhin du de bzhin gshegs pa dgra
182a8(mdo sde): bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas kyang srid pa'i rgya mtsho las mngon par 'phags te/ chos kyi dbyings na mkha'i spyod yul la gnas nas/ ye shes kyi 'od zer
182b1(mdo sde): bye ba khrag khrig 'bum phrag grangs med pa btang bas/ phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten gyi khams rab 'byams thams cad snang ba'i sbyin par mdzad cing / sems can khams
182b2(mdo sde): cad kyi ma rig pa'i mun pa mun nag dang / rab rib dang / ling tog rnams rnam par sel bar mdzad/ nyon mongs pa'i 'dam rdzab dang / rnyog pa thams cad skems par mdzad//
182b3(mdo sde): yun ring po nas gnyid kyis log pa'i sems can gyi khams ni sad par mdzad/ sems can thams cad kyi dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad ni skye bar mdzad/ sems can thams cad kyi
182b4(mdo sde): dge ba'i rtsa ba tshogs thams cad ni yongs su smin par mdzad/ dge ba'i rtsa ba'i sgo thams cad ni rab tu 'joms par mdzad do// dus gcig tu de'i mdzad pa thams cad 'byung
182b5(mdo sde): yang gnas nas kyang mi g.yo zhing / 'jam dpal de bzhin gshegs pa ni mi rtog parnam par mi rtog ste/ 'on kyang ma 'dres pa chos dang ldan pa'i phyir lhun gyis
182b6(mdo sde): grub cing rnam par mi rtog par de'i mdzad pa de lta bu de 'byung ngo // 'jam dpal de ltar de bzhin gshegs pa ni lhun gyis grub cing rnam par mi rtog par sems can
182b7(mdo sde): yongs su smin par mdzad pa'i gnas kyang dge ba'i bshes gnyen gyis yongs su zin pa las byung / 'jam dpal dge ba'i bshes gnyen gyis yongs su zin pa'i byang
182b8(mdo sde): chub sems dpa' ni chos rab tu rnam par 'byed pa dang / spyod pa mkhas par 'gyur te/ de la chos rnams la 'di ltar spyod do// mig ni gzugs kyi dmigs pa'i rgyu ma yin/
183a1(mdo sde): gzugs kyi mig ni dmigs pa'i rgyu ma yin la/ dmigs pa'i rgyu rkyen nyid kyi rnam par shes pa 'byung ste/ rnam par shes pa de yang mig
183a2(mdo sde): las kyang ma byung / gzugs las kyang ma byung zhing rnam par shes pa de ni/ byung nas nig la zhu zhing mi gnas pa'o// rna ba dang / sna dang / lce dang / lus kyang de bzhin no// yid kyang
183a3(mdo sde): chos kyi rkyen ma yin zhing / chos kyang yid kyi rkyen ma yin la/ dmigs pa'i rgyu rkyen nyid kyis kyang rnam par shes pa 'byung ste/ rnam par shes pa de ni yid las kyang ma byung / chos rnams
183a4(mdo sde): las kyang ma byung yid kyi rnam par shes pa de ni byung nas kyang zhig la/ zhu zhing mi gnas pa'o// de bzhin du dge ba'i rtsa ba yang byang chub kyi rkyen ma yin/ byang chub kyang dge ba'i rtsa
183a5(mdo sde): ba'i rkyen ma yin mod kyi dpag tu med grangs med pa dag phyir rnyil bar byed do// sangs rgyas kyi rnam par rol 'bye ba khrag khrig 'bum phrag dpag tu med grangs med pa dag
183a6(mdo sde): rab tu shes so// nga rgyal gyi ri dpag tu med pa dag tum par 'jig par byed do// phra dog dang ser sna'i rgyal mtshan dpag tu med grangs med pa dag snyil bar byed do// sred
183a7(mdo sde): pa'i chu klung dpag tu med grangs med pa dag skems par byed do// skye ba'i rgya mtsho dpag tu med grangs med pa dag las rgal bar byed do// bdud kyi nags pa dpag tu med
183a8(mdo sde): grangs med pa dag gtsang ngo // nyi zla rnams dang / brgya byin dang / tshangs pa dang / 'jig rten skyong ba rnams kyi gzi brjid zil gyis mnan te 'dug go// sangs rgyas kyi zhing
183b1(mdo sde): nas sangs rgyas kyi zhing du 'gro'o// sems can dmyal ba dang / dud 'gro dang / yi dgas dang / gshin rje'i 'jig rten du skyes pa'i sems can rnams kyi skyabs
183b2(mdo sde): su 'gyur ro// sangs rgyas rnams dang byang chub sems dpa' rnams dang yang phrad par 'gyur ro// rgya mtsho'i phyag rgya zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin kyang thob po// chos thams
183b3(mdo sde): cad yang dag par 'du ba zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin kyang thob po// chos thams cad la dbang byed zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin kyang thob po// rnam par bkod pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge
183b4(mdo sde): 'dzin kyang thob po// rin po che 'byung ba zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin kyang thob po// dga' bar byed pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin kyang thob po// pad+ma bkod pa zhes bya ba'i ting
183b5(mdo sde): nge 'dzin kyang thob po// namakha' mdzod ces bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin kyang thob po// 'jig rten thams cad kyi rjes su song ba zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin kyang thob po// dam
183b6(mdo sde): pa'i chos pad+ma dkar po zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin kyang thob po// yul la dbang byed pa zhes bya ba'i tingange 'dzin kyang thob po// rnam pa dang sems la dbang byed pa zhes
183b7(mdo sde): bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin kyang thob po// seng ge bsgyings pa zhes bya ba'i tingange 'dzin kyang thob po// nyi ma'i sgron ma zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin kyang thob po// mtha' yas
183b8(mdo sde): 'khyil pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin kyang thob po// rab tu g.yo ba'i rjes su song ba zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin kyang thob po// rdo rje dkyil 'khor zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin kyang
184a1(mdo sde): rdo rje'i rgyal mtshan zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin kyang thob bo// rdo rje lta bu zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin kyang thob po// rdo rje lte ba zhes bya ba'i ting nge
184a2(mdo sde): 'dzin kyang thob po// sa 'dzin zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin kyang thob po// lhun po'i sgron ma zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin kyang thob po// lhun po'i rgyal mtshan zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin
184a3(mdo sde): kyang thob po// rin po che'i 'dzod ces bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin kyang thob po// sems dbang byed pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin kyang thob po// sems can thams cad kyi sems la
184a4(mdo sde): dbang byed pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin kyang thob bo// spyod pa thams cad kyi yul la nges par 'byung ba zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin kyang thob po// sna tshogs snang ba'i spobs pa
184a5(mdo sde): zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin kyang thob po// ltar mi mthong ba zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin kyang thob po// chos thams cad la rnam par lta ba zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin kyang thob po//
184a6(mdo sde): rnam par rol pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin kyang thob po// mngon par shes pa thams cad las nges par skyes pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin kyang thob po// bdud kyi dkyil 'khor
184a7(mdo sde): rnam par mjoms pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin kyang zab po// gzugs thams cad kun du ston pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin kyang thong po// gzugs thams cad khyab
184a8(mdo sde): pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin kyang thob po// yul rnam par 'jig pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin kyang thob po// spyod pa thams cad la 'jug pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin
184b1(mdo sde): kyang thob bo// shes rab sgron ma zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin kyang thob bo// mngon sum du byang chub snang ba zhes bya ba ting nge 'dzin kyang thob bo// so so yang dag par
184b2(mdo sde): rig pa chen po bstan pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin kyang thob bo// yon tan gyi rnam pa thams cad la 'jug pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin kyang thob po// chos thams cad
184b3(mdo sde): 'dul bar rnam par nges par bstan pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin kyang thob po// rab tu zhi ba rnam par nges pa'i cho 'phrul zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin kyang thob po// dpa'
184b4(mdo sde): bar 'gro ba zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin kyang thob po// zab cing bstan pa'i rgya mtsho'i chu'i dus rlabs zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin kyang thob bo// de dag la sogs pa'i ting
184b5(mdo sde): nge 'dzin bye ba khrag khrig 'bum khrag grangs med pa dag thob bo// sangs rgyas kyi sku dang / kha dog mtha' yas pa yongasu 'grub pa'i gzungs kyang thob po// ye shes
184b6(mdo sde): dang ldan pa zhes bya ba'i gzungs kyang thob po// sgra dbyangs rnam par dag pa zhes bya ba'i gzungs kyang thob po// mi zad pa za ma tog ces bya ba'i grezungs kyang thob po//
184b7(mdo sde): mtha' yas 'khyil pa zhes bya ba'i gzungs kyang thob bo// rgya mtsho phyag rgya zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin kyang thob po// pad+ma dkar po bkod pa zhes bya ba'i gzungs kyang thob
184b8(mdo sde): go// chags pa med pa'i sgor 'jug pa zhes bya ba'i gzungs kyang thob bo// so so yang dag par rig pa rnam par nges pa la 'jug pa zhes bya ba'i gzungs kyang thob bo//
185a1(mdo sde): sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis brlabs pa zhes bya ba'i gzungs kyang thob bo// sangs rgyas kyi sku dang kha dog mtha' yas yongs su
185a2(mdo sde): 'grub pa zhes bya ba'i gzungs kyang thob ste// de dag la sogs pa gzungs bye ba khrag khrig 'bum phrag grangs med pa dag kyang thob bo// chos thams cad la spyod pa'i
185a3(mdo sde): khyad par nyid kyang thob po// chos thams cad la gzhan rag ma lus pa'i shes pa yang thob po// chos thams cad la som nyid gcod pa nyid kyang thob po// sangs rgyas kyi rna
185a4(mdo sde): par rol pa stong phrag grangs med pa dag kyang thob po// sems can thams cad kyi spyod pa'i bye brag la mkhas pa yang thob po// 'jam dpal dper na/ ri'i rgyal po re rab
185a5(mdo sde): ni/ ri thams cad zil gyis mnan nas/ lam me lhan ne lhang nge'o// 'jam dpal de bzhin du chos kyi rnam grangs 'di la mos pa'i byang chub sems dpa' yang sems can
185a6(mdo sde): thams cad kyi dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad zil gyis mnan nas/ lam me lhan ne lhang nge'o// de nas 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pas/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa'
185a7(mdo sde): chen po sgrib pa thams cad rnam par sel ba la 'di skad ces smras so// kye'i rgyal ba'i sras byang chub sems dpa' gang dag la mos pas/ yon tan gyi khyad par 'di dag dang /
185a8(mdo sde): gzhan dag kyang thob pa'i chos kyi bye brag gzhan dag kyang yod dam/ de skad ces smras pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' sgrib pa thams cad rnam par sel bas/ 'jam dpal
185b1(mdo sde): gnon nur gyur pa la 'di skad ces smras so// 'jas dpal byang chub sems dang 'gad dag la mos na/ yon tan gyi khyad par 'di dag dang / gnan dpag tu med pa dag kyang bag/
185b2(mdo sde): pa'i chos lnga po 'di dag ste/ lnga gang zhe na/ chos thams cad gnyen po med pa dang / ma skyes pa dang / ma 'gags pa dang / brjod du med par mos pa dang / rtag tu rgyun mi 'chad
185b3(mdo sde): par skad cig gcig la de bzhin gshegs pa'i spyod pa dang / spyod las la 'jug pa'i gnas 'dzam bu'i gling gi rdul las kyang lhag pa dag la lhun gyis grub cing rnam par mi
185b4(mdo sde): rtog par mos pa dang / seng ge bran bzangs kyi bu'i rtogs pa brjod pa dang / sems can yongs su smin par byas pa de/ bcom ldan 'das shAkya thub pas bskal pa gang ga'i
185b5(mdo sde): klung gi bye ma snyed nas mngon par rdzogs par sangs rgyas de mdzad par mos pa dang / mar me mdzad kyis lung ston pa nas bzung ste/ mngon par rdzogs par byang chub pa'i bar der/
185b6(mdo sde): bcom ldan 'das shAkya thub pas byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa gang yin pa de thams cad sangs rgyas kyi yul gyi mthas klas pa'i bskal pa nas// mngon par rdzogs par sangs
185b7(mdo sde): rgyas nas bstan pa yin par mos pa dang / shA thub pas bstan nas/ sems can yongs su smin par byas pa gang yin pa de/ sangs rgyas kyi yul gyim thas klas pa'i bas/
185b8(mdo sde): pa nas/ bcom ldan 'das shAkya thub pa mngon par rdzogs par sangs rgyas nas mdzad pa yin par mos pa ste/ 'jam dpal lnga po de dag ni byang chub sems dpas gang dag la
186a1(mdo sde): mos pas yon tan gyi khyad par 'di dag dang / gzhan dpag tu med pa de dag kyang thob pa yin no// 'jam dpal rigs kyi bu 'am/ rigs

186a3(mdo sde): nyin cig bzhin du lha'i zas ro brgya dang ldan pa dang / lha'i gos dag byin te de ltar byin pa bskal pa gang ga'i klung gi bye ma snyed dag tu byin pa bas/ 'jam dpal rigs kyi bu 'am
186a4(mdo sde): rigs kyi bu mo gzhan gang zhig gis/ rang sangs rgyas gcig la nyi ma gcig zan byin na/ de ni de bas bsod nams ches grangs med par bskyed do// 'jam dpal rigs kyi bu/

206a6(mdo sde): mtha' yas bar du bshad na yang // chung zad tsam yang yongs su brjod mi 'gyur// sa bzhi dag las rdul ni blangs pa bzhin// de ltar rgyal po skyes mchog
206a7(mdo sde): kyi kyang // byang chub sems kyi phan yon 'di thos nang // myur du blo gros dma' ba kun spongs la// byang chub phyir ni rgya chen sems bskyed cig/ 'jig rten 'dren pa gser

206b1(mdo sde): kyi rnam smin bstan pa yin// bsod nams de la gal te gzugs yod na// zhing rnams gang gi 'ji snyed gang byas kyang // de dag gang bas ma tsam zad pa med// rjes su/
206b2(mdo sde): bstan pa 'di 'dra thos nas kyang // rgyal po gtso bo'i sems ni dga'agyur te// sor mo bcu'i thal mo sbyar byas nas// sangs rgyas phyag 'tshal zhes ni tshig tu smras//
206b3(mdo sde): byang chub phyir ni bdag gis sems bskyed de// bdag ni sangs rgyas chos rje 'grub par shog/ byang chub rdul bral 'das ma byas rtogs nas// sems can gang gi bye
206b4(mdo sde): snyed dgrol bar bgyi// sangs rgyas sku des tshigs bcad 'di brjod nas// de tshe rgyal ba'i gtso bo dga' gyur pa// shes nas stong gsum thams cad rang gsos te//
206b5(mdo sde): ngang pa'i rgyal po bzhin du mkha' las song // rgyal po gser mdog sems ni dad gyur nas// bu dang bu mo de bzhin chung ma dang // rgyal po dang ni tshong dpon khyim bad/
206b6(mdo sde): rnams// sangs rgyas la ni phyag 'tshal 'dod zhes bos// bye ba brgya phrag drug bcus yongs bskor cing // me tog rnams dang phreng dang gdug spos thogs//
206b7(mdo sde): sangs rgyas ga la bar ni gnyi rgyud song // zhabs la phyag 'tshal nas ni phyogs cig 'dug/ de bzhin bu dang bu mo chung ma dang // blon po dang ni khyim bdag tshong dpon dang //
206b8(mdo sde): rgyal po gzhan dang de bzhin 'khor gyi rnams// de dag kyang ni phyag 'tshal gus pas 'khod// lha rnams kyis kyang bar snang thams cad khyab// sil snyen dkrol zhing
207a1(mdo sde): me tog char pa phab// gser gyi mdog de yul gyi mis bskor nas// thazal mo sbyar byas sangs rgyas zhu bar byed// stobs bcu ldan
207a2(mdo sde): pa dpag med lha yi lha// mi 'dal kha lo bsgyur ba khyod la zhu// gang gis byang chub sems ni brtan por bskyed// de yi bsod nams ji tsam bskyed 'gyur lags//
207a3(mdo sde): bcom ldan ji ltar spyod pa spyad bgyis na// bskal pa mang por sdug bsngal mi mthong bar// nges par bde dang bde blag tshim gyur pas// byang chub bdud rtsi mya ngan med
207a4(mdo sde): par rtogs// bdag gzhan rkang lag btang yang mi 'tshal zhing // mgo dang rang sha btsal yang mi 'tshal bar// bdag ni nges par bder gnas spyod pa yi// thab
207a5(mdo sde): 'dir thub pas bdag la stan du gsol// rtag tu bde dang bde ldan par shog/ nams kyang bdag lus sdug bsngal ma gyur cig/ byams dang bzod dang dul dang
207a6(mdo sde): sdom pa la// gnas nas bdag gi byang chub mchog reg mchog/ le lo ma mchis kun nas brtson 'grus dang // rtag tu bslab pa rnams kyang bzhig mi bgyi// 'dren pa

207b1(mdo sde): kyai sa'i bdag po ma nyan par bgyi// bden pa'i rgyu'i bsod nams khyod la bshad// bslab pa'ang bshad kyis de phyir nga las nyon// gang gis stong gsum rin chen gang
207b2(mdo sde): gang byas la// stobs bcu mnga' ba rnams la 'bul byed pa// de bas byang chub tu ni smon byed pa// bsod nams shin du mang po 'phel bar 'gyur// gang gis zhing
207b3(mdo sde): rnams gang gi bye ma snyed// rin chen gang bar byas nas sbyin pa byin// de bas byang chub tu ni smon lam 'bum byed pa// bsod nams shin du mang po 'phel bar 'gyur//
207b4(mdo sde): gang gi bskal pa bye ba khrag khrig tu// sems can thams cad la ni mchod par byed// de bas byang chub tu ni smon byed pa// bsod nams shin tu mang po 'phel bar 'gyur// /
207b5(mdo sde): gal te sems can thams cad dgra bcom gyur// ye shes dbang thob gyur pa de dag la// bsod nams 'dod pa'i gang zag la la zhig/ bskal pa khrag khrig par
207b6(mdo sde): du mchod par byed// gang gis snying rje bskyed nas byang chub tu// rgya chen sems ni bskyed par byed 'gyur te// sems can la la zhig gis byang chub tu// sems kyi gtso
207b7(mdo sde): bo bskyed pa byas nas kyang // gom pa bdun ni bor ba'i bsod nams 'di// de bas khyad par 'phags par 'gyur ba yin// gal te sems can mtha' dag sang
207b8(mdo sde): rgyas te// stobs la mtha' yas ldan pa nyid gyur la// ji ltar sngon gyi 'khor ba'i bskal pa'i bar// sems can cig pus mchod pa byas pa dang / mkhas pa'i
208a1(mdo sde): mi ni gang yang rung ba yis// byang chub mchog tu sems ni bskyed nas kyang // me tog gcig pu phul ba'i bsod nams 'di//

208a3(mdo sde): pa ni/ nams kyang zad par 'gyur ba ma yin no// rigs kyi bu 'di ltar bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa gser bzang 'od des rgyal po gser mdog de la 'di

208a5(mdo sde): rdzogs pa'i byang chub mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya bar 'gyur la/ sdug bsngal ba dang / yid mi bde bar yang mi 'gyur ro// chos cig po gang zhe na/ 'di lta
208a6(mdo sde): ste/ bag phod pa ste/ rgyal po chen po byang chub sems dpa' bag yod pa ni myur du bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub mngon par rdzogs par 'chang bar 'gyur ro//

208b1(mdo sde): la brten cing bsnyen bkur byed pa dang / chos la gus pa dang / zos pa mang pos chog shes pa dang / gzhan dag dang chos kyi bgo bsha' byed pa dang / zang zing med
208b2(mdo sde): par chos ston pa dang / sbyangs pa'i yon tan dang / yo byad sbyangs pa rnams mi stong pa dang / 'dod pa nyung ba dang / chog shes pa dang / nga rgyal bcom pa dang /

208b7(mdo sde): nges par 'byung bar byed pa dang / mngon par 'byung ba dang / dge sbyong gi tshul la rgyun du dga' ba dang / gsong por smra ba dang / bzhin khro gnyer med pa dang / chos
208b8(mdo sde): thams cad skye ba med pa dang / 'gag pa med pa la 'dzud pa dang / chos thams cad na mkha' dang 'dra bar rtog pa 'di ni byang chub sems dpa'i bag yod pa zhes bya'o//
209a1(mdo sde): rgyal po chen po gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa'i bag yod pa ni/ 'di lta ste/ nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas kyi sems dang / dmigs
